 Nasira Sharmanasira Sharma is one of those story writers who have a keen grasp on the culture, society, literature and politics of not only Indians but other Asian countries, especially Muslim countries
 unhen in vishyon kaa visheshgy bhi mana jaataa he

 1
 Apply candles - During festive season, you can burn candles to give your home a soft look

 Decorate with ribbons - buy white, red and green ribbons this Christmas

 teble ko decorat karen-aap apane ghar main maujuud teble ko christmas ko roshni kii tarah floating candal se roshan kar sakate hai

 Install Santa Claus - You can hang small Santa Claus available in markets everywhere to give Christmas touch to your home and office
